Per thread: for c_in in 0..Cin-1: for kd in 0..K-1: // Check d validity d = 2*(d_idx) + 1, where d_idx is the index among odd coordinates. d_in_full = d + 1 - 2*kd = 2*d_idx + 2 - 2*kd = 2*(d_idx + 1 - kd). d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd. if d_in < 0 or >= D_in: continue. // Similarly for h and w: h = 2*h_idx + 1, h_in = h_idx + 1 - kh. w = 2*w_idx + 1, w_in = w_idx + 1 - kw. if all valid: x_addr = ((b*Cin + c_in)*D_in + d_in)*H_in*W_in + h_in*W_in + w_in w_addr = ((c_in*Cout + c_out)*K + kd)*K*K + kh*K + kw acc += x[x_addr] * weight[w_addr] Wait, does this capture all non-zero output? Let's verify with the small example: D_out=5, D_in=2. Odd d idx: 0 -> d=1, 1 -> d=3. For d_idx=0, d=1: kd=0: d_in = 0+1-0 = 1 (valid, <2) kd=1: d_in = 0+1-1 = 0 (valid) kd=2: d_in = 0+1-2 = -1 (invalid) For d_idx=1, d=3: kd=0: d_in = 1+1-0 = 2 (invalid, >=2) kd=1: d_in = 1+1-1 = 1 (valid) kd=2: d_in = 1+1-2 = 0 (valid) So at d_idx=1, only kd=1,2 are valid. This matches the mapping from the scatter view: For d_in=0, valid kd are 1,2 producing d=1,3. For d_in=1, valid kd are 1,2 producing d=3,5 (but d=5 is out of bounds for D_out=5). Wait, scatter view said d_in=1, kd=0 => d=1, kd=1 => d=3, kd=2 => d=5 (oob). In the gather view above, d_idx=0 (d=1) gets contributions from kd=0 (d_in=1) and kd=1 (d_in=0). But scatter view says d=1 comes from d_in=1, kd=0, and also from d_in=? kd=1 gives d=1*2+2*1-1=3. Wait, no. Let's recompute scatter: d = d_in * stride + kd * dilation - padding For d_in=0, kd=0: d = 0*2 + 0*2 - 1 = -1 (oob) kd=1: d = 0*2 + 1*2 -1 = 1 (valid) kd=2: d = 0*2 + 2*2 -1 = 3 (valid) For d_in=1, kd=0: d = 2 + 0 -1 = 1 (valid) kd=1: d = 2 + 2 -1 = 3 (valid) kd=2: d = 2 + 4 -1 = 5 (oob) So output at d=1 receives contributions from: - d_in=0, kd=1 - d_in=1, kd=0 Output at d=3 receives contributions from: - d_in=0, kd=2 - d_in=1, kd=1 In the gather view with d=1: d_idx = (d-1)/2 = 0. kd=0: d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd = 1. This corresponds to d_in=1, kd=0. kd=1: d_in = 0+1-1 = 0. This corresponds to d_in=0, kd=1. kd=2: d_in = -1. Invalid. Yes! It matches perfectly. So the simplified gather kernel for odd coordinates only is: d_idx = ... d = 2*d_idx + 1 d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd This automatically handles the valid range and the correct mapping. Similarly for h and w. This is a GREAT simplification. It eliminates all modulo and conditional checks for parity. Edge cases: D_out can be even or odd. For D_out=33, d ranges 0..32, odd d: 1..31 (16 values). d_idx: 0..15. d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd. For d_idx=15, kd=0 => d_in=16 (invalid, since D_in=16, valid 0..15). kd=1 => d_in=15 (valid). kd=2 => d_in=14 (valid). For d_idx=0, kd=0 => d_in=1. kd=1 => d_in=0. kd=2 => d_in=-1 (invalid). When does d_in become invalid for kd=0? d_idx + 1 >= D_in => d_idx >= D_in - 1 = 15. When does it become invalid for kd=2? d_idx + 1 - 2 < 0 => d_idx < 1 => d_idx = 0. So only at edges. For D_in=16, d_idx ranges 0..15. At d_idx=0: valid kd=1,2? Wait, kd=0 gives d_in=1 (valid!), kd=1 gives d_in=0 (valid!), kd=2 gives d_in=-1 (invalid). So 2 valid. At d_idx=15: kd=0 gives 16 (invalid), kd=1 gives 15 (valid), kd=2 gives 14 (valid). So 2 valid. At d_idx=1: kd=0 gives 2, kd=1 gives 1, kd=2 gives 0. All 3 valid. At d_idx=14: kd=0 gives 15, kd=1 gives 14, kd=2 gives 13. All 3 valid. So most positions have 3 valid kd. Same for h and w. This means per output element, ~3*3*3 = 27 kernel positions are processed for the central region, but the edge regions have fewer (e.g., 2x3x3, etc.). Since D_out//2 = 16 and D_in = 16, the "edge" in d is only at idx 0 and 15. For h_out=65, H_in=32, valid h_idx 0..31. Wait, H_out//2 = 32. h_idx ranges 0..31. h_in = h_idx + 1 - kh. At h_idx=0: kh=0 => h_in=1, kh=1 => 0, kh=2 => -1 (invalid). So 2 valid. At h_idx=31: kh=0 => 32 (invalid since H_in=32, valid 0..31), kh=1 => 31, kh=2 => 30. So 2 valid. So edges in each dimension have 2 valid positions for that dimension. Interior (h_idx 1..30) have 3 valid. Since interior is large, average valid kernel positions per output is still close to 27. Wait, that's more than my earlier estimate of 8. Why? Because I mistakenly thought only odd coordinates were non-zero, but then for each odd coordinate, there are up to 3 valid kd values. But wait, earlier I calculated that for fixed d and kd, d_in is determined and we need 0 <= d_in < D_in. For d=1 (d_idx=0), kd=0 gives d_in=1, kd=1 gives d_in=0, kd=2 gives d_in=-1. So 2 valid kd values. For d=3 (d_idx=1), kd=0 => d_in=2, kd=1=>1, kd=2=>0. 3 valid. So along d, average valid kd is (2 + 30*3 + 2) / 32 = 94/32 ≈ 2.9375. Similarly h and w: (2 + 30*3 + 2)/32 = same. Average valid positions: 2.9375^3 ≈ 25.3. Cin=32, so FMAs per output: 32 * 25.3 ≈ 810. Total FMAs: 17.8M * 810 ≈ 14.4B FMAs. This is about 3x more than my previous estimate. Because I forgot that d_idx range is D_out//2 = 16, not D_out. Wait, D_out=33, D_out//2=16. d_idx ranges 0..15. Number of valid kd per d_idx: At d_idx=0: kd=0,1 valid => 2. At d_idx=15: kd=1,2 valid => 2. At d_idx=1..14: kd=0,1,2 valid => 3. (14 values) Average = (2*2 + 14*3) / 16 = (4+42)/16 = 46/16 = 2.875. Ah! For D_in=16, H_in=32: d_idx count = 16. h_idx count = 32. Average valid kd = 2.875. Average valid kh = (2*2 + 30*3) / 32 = 94/32 = 2.9375. Same for kw. Average valid kernel positions = 2.875 * 2.9375 * 2.9375 = 24.79. FMAs per non-zero output = 32 * 24.79 ≈ 793. Total FMAs = 16*64*16*32*32 * 793 = 16,777,216 * 793 ≈ 13.3 billion. Still, 13.3B FMAs, on a GPU with say 20 TFLOPS = 20,000 GFLOPS, that's 0.66 ms if compute bound. If memory bound: each non-zero output reads 793 x values + 793 w values = ~1586 floats = 6.3KB? No, that's not right. Actually, per output, we read x 793 times and weight 793 times. But that's per thread, not total memory traffic. The total unique x elements used: roughly B*Cin*D_in*H_in*W_in * average reads per x element. Each x element is read by up to 27 output positions (one per kernel position). So total x reads = 16*32*16*32*32 * 27 ≈ 226M reads. Total weight reads = Cin*Cout*K^3 * B * some reuse factor. Each weight is used by B * D_in * H_in * W_in elements. So total weight reads = 32*64*27 * 16*16*32*32 = 55,296 * 262,144 ≈ 14.5B reads. But weights are cached and reused across threads. If weights stay in L2/L1 cache, x reads are the main memory bandwidth. 226M floats = 904 MB. If bandwidth is 1 TB/s, that's < 1 ms. Plus weight reads from HBM might be a few GB. So total memory traffic maybe a few GB, which at 1 TB/s is a few ms. Compute is ~13B FMAs = ~0.7 ms at 20 TFLOPS. So it's likely compute bound or balanced. A simple gather kernel where each thread computes one non-zero output element and loops over c_in, kd,kh,kw should be decent. But can it beat cuDNN? Not sure. We can optimize further with tiling: - Tile c_in across blocks or shared memory. - Use vectorized loads for x. But given the complexity, let's start with a straightforward gather kernel on the reduced grid and see if correctness passes. Then measure performance. If it's not faster than cuDNN, I'll need to optimize more. Write the kernel: cuda_source = ''' #include <torch/extension.h> #include <cuda.h> #include <cuda_runtime.h> __global__ void conv_transpose3d_forward_kernel( const float* __restrict__ x, const float* __restrict__ weight, float* __restrict__ out, int B, int Cin, int Cout, int D_in, int H_in, int W_in, int D_out, int H_out, int W_out, int K, int stride, int padding, int dilation) { // Compute number of odd positions per spatial dim int D_odd = D_out / 2; int H_odd = H_out / 2; int W_odd = W_out / 2; int total = B * Cout * D_odd * H_odd * W_odd; int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x; if (idx >= total) return; int tmp = idx; int w_idx = tmp % W_odd; tmp /= W_odd; int h_idx = tmp % H_odd; tmp /= H_odd; int d_idx = tmp % D_odd; tmp /= D_odd; int c_out = tmp % Cout; tmp /= Cout; int b = tmp; int w = 2 * w_idx + 1; int h = 2 * h_idx + 1; int d = 2 * d_idx + 1; float acc = 0.0f; // The mapping for odd output coordinates: // d = 2*d_idx + 1, and from scatter: d = d_in*stride + kd*dilation - padding // With stride=2, padding=1, dilation=2: // 2*d_idx+1 = d_in*2 + kd*2 - 1 // 2*d_idx+2 = 2*(d_in + kd) // d_idx + 1 = d_in + kd // => d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd // This holds specifically for stride=2, padding=1, dilation=2. // We'll keep generic checks but use this simplification for common params. // Generic approach: for (int c_in = 0; c_in < Cin; ++c_in) { for (int kd = 0; kd < K; ++kd) { int d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd; if (d_in < 0 || d_in >= D_in) continue; for (int kh = 0; kh < K; ++kh) { int h_in = h_idx + 1 - kh; if (h_in < 0 || h_in >= H_in) continue; for (int kw = 0; kw < K; ++kw) { int w_in = w_idx + 1 - kw; if (w_in < 0 || w_in >= W_in) continue; float x_val = x[(((b * Cin + c_in) * D_in + d_in) * H_in + h_in) * W_in + w_in]; float w_val = weight[(((c_in * Cout + c_out) * K + kd) * K + kh) * K + kw]; acc += x_val * w_val; } } } } out[(((b * Cout + c_out) * D_out + d) * H_out + h) * W_out + w] = acc; } // Also need a generic fallback kernel for other parameter combinations // but since the problem says fixed args, maybe only this one matters. // Still provide fallback. __global__ void conv_transpose3d_forward_generic_kernel( const float* __restrict__ x, const float* __restrict__ weight, float* __restrict__ out, int B, int Cin, int Cout, int D_in, int H_in, int W_in, int D_out, int H_out, int W_out, int K, int stride, int padding, int dilation) { int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x; int total = B * Cout * D_out * H_out * W_out; if (idx >= total) return; int w = idx % W_out; idx /= W_out; int h = idx % H_out; idx /= H_out; int d = idx % D_out; idx /= D_out; int c_out = idx % Cout; idx /= Cout; int b = idx; float acc = 0.0f; for (int c_in = 0; c_in < Cin; ++c_in) { for (int kd = 0; kd < K; ++kd) { int d_in_full = d + padding - dilation * kd; if (d_in_full % stride != 0) continue; int d_in = d_in_full / stride; if (d_in < 0 || d_in >= D_in) continue; for (int kh = 0; kh < K; ++kh) { int h_in_full = h + padding - dilation * kh; if (h_in_full % stride != 0) continue; int h_in = h_in_full / stride; if (h_in < 0 || h_in >= H_in) continue; for (int kw = 0; kw < K; ++kw) { int w_in_full = w + padding - dilation * kw; if (w_in_full % stride != 0) continue; int w_in = w_in_full / stride; if (w_in < 0 || w_in >= W_in) continue; float x_val = x[(((b * Cin + c_in) * D_in + d_in) * H_in + h_in) * W_in + w_in]; float w_val = weight[(((c_in * Cout + c_out) * K + kd) * K + kh) * K + kw]; acc += x_val * w_val; } } } } out[(((b * Cout + c_out) * D_out + d) * H_out + h) * W_out + w] = acc; } torch::Tensor conv_transpose3d_forward( torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor weight, int64_t stride, int64_t padding, int64_t dilation) { int B = x.size(0); int Cin = x.size(1); int D_in = x.size(2); int H_in = x.size(3); int W_in = x.size(4); int Cout = weight.size(1); int K = weight.size(2); int D_out = (D_in - 1) * stride - 2 * padding + dilation * (K - 1) + 1; int H_out = (H_in - 1) * stride - 2 * padding + dilation * (K - 1) + 1; int W_out = (W_in - 1) * stride - 2 * padding + dilation * (K - 1) + 1; auto out = torch::zeros({B, Cout, D_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options()); if (stride == 2 && padding == 1 && dilation == 2) { int D_odd = D_out / 2; int H_odd = H_out / 2; int W_odd = W_out / 2; int total = B * Cout * D_odd * H_odd * W_odd; const int threads = 256; const int blocks = (total + threads - 1) / threads; conv_transpose3d_forward_kernel<<<blocks, threads>>>( x.data_ptr<float>(), weight.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>(), B, Cin, Cout, D_in, H_in, W_in, D_out, H_out, W_out, K, (int)stride, (int)padding, (int)dilation); } else { int total = B * Cout * D_out * H_out * W_out; const int threads = 256; const int blocks = (total + threads - 1) / threads; conv_transpose3d_forward_generic_kernel<<<blocks, threads>>>( x.data_ptr<float>(), weight.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>(), B, Cin, Cout, D_in, H_in, W_in, D_out, H_out, W_out, K, (int)stride, (int)padding, (int)dilation); } return out; } PYBIND11_MODULE(TORCH_EXTENSION_NAME, m) { m.def("conv_transpose3d_forward", &conv_transpose3d_forward, "ConvTranspose3D forward"); } ''' Now, how to compile this with `torch.utils.cpp_extension.load` using `use_ninja=False`? import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cuda_sources = r"""
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>

template <int K>
__global__ void conv_transpose3d_forward_specialized_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    const float* __restrict__ weight,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B,
    int Cin,
    int Cout,
    int D_in,
    int H_in,
    int W_in,
    int D_out,
    int H_out,
    int W_out)
{
    int D_odd = D_out / 2;
    int H_odd = H_out / 2;
    int W_odd = W_out / 2;
    int total = B * Cout * D_odd * H_odd * W_odd;
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    if (idx >= total) return;

    int tmp = idx;
    int w_idx = tmp % W_odd; tmp /= W_odd;
    int h_idx = tmp % H_odd; tmp /= H_odd;
    int d_idx = tmp % D_odd; tmp /= D_odd;
    int c_out = tmp % Cout; tmp /= Cout;
    int b = tmp;

    int w = 2 * w_idx + 1;
    int h = 2 * h_idx + 1;
    int d = 2 * d_idx + 1;

    float acc = 0.0f;

    for (int c_in = 0; c_in < Cin; ++c_in) {
        #pragma unroll
        for (int kd = 0; kd < K; ++kd) {
            int d_in = d_idx + 1 - kd;
            if (d_in < 0 || d_in >= D_in) continue;
            #pragma unroll
            for (int kh = 0; kh < K; ++kh) {
                int h_in = h_idx + 1 - kh;
                if (h_in < 0 || h_in >= H_in) continue;
                #pragma unroll
                for (int kw = 0; kw < K; ++kw) {
                    int w_in = w_idx + 1 - kw;
                    if (w_in < 0 || w_in >= W_in) continue;
                    float x_val = x[(((b * Cin + c_in) * D_in + d_in) * H_in + h_in) * W_in + w_in];
                    float w_val = weight[(((c_in * Cout + c_out) * K + kd) * K + kh) * K + kw];
                    acc += x_val * w_val;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    out[(((b * Cout + c_out) * D_out + d) * H_out + h) * W_out + w] = acc;
}

__global__ void conv_transpose3d_forward_generic_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    const float* __restrict__ weight,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B,
    int Cin,
    int Cout,
    int D_in,
    int H_in,
    int W_in,
    int D_out,
    int H_out,
    int W_out,
    int K,
    int stride,
    int padding,
    int dilation)
{
    int idx = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
    int total = B * Cout * D_out * H_out * W_out;
    if (idx >= total) return;

    int w = idx % W_out; idx /= W_out;
    int h = idx % H_out; idx /= H_out;
    int d = idx % D_out; idx /= D_out;
    int c_out = idx % Cout; idx /= Cout;
    int b = idx;

    float acc = 0.0f;
    for (int c_in = 0; c_in < Cin; ++c_in) {
        for (int kd = 0; kd < K; ++kd) {
            int d_in_full = d + padding - dilation * kd;
            if (d_in_full % stride != 0) continue;
            int d_in = d_in_full / stride;
            if (d_in < 0 || d_in >= D_in) continue;
            for (int kh = 0; kh < K; ++kh) {
                int h_in_full = h + padding - dilation * kh;
                if (h_in_full % stride != 0) continue;
                int h_in = h_in_full / stride;
                if (h_in < 0 || h_in >= H_in) continue;
                for (int kw = 0; kw < K; ++kw) {
                    int w_in_full = w + padding - dilation * kw;
                    if (w_in_full % stride != 0) continue;
                    int w_in = w_in_full / stride;
                    if (w_in < 0 || w_in >= W_in) continue;
                    float x_val = x[(((b * Cin + c_in) * D_in + d_in) * H_in + h_in) * W_in + w_in];
                    float w_val = weight[(((c_in * Cout + c_out) * K + kd) * K + kh) * K + kw];
                    acc += x_val * w_val;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    out[(((b * Cout + c_out) * D_out + d) * H_out + h) * W_out + w] = acc;
}

torch::Tensor conv_transpose3d_forward(
    torch::Tensor x,
    torch::Tensor weight,
    int64_t stride,
    int64_t padding,
    int64_t dilation)
{
    int B = x.size(0);
    int Cin = x.size(1);
    int D_in = x.size(2);
    int H_in = x.size(3);
    int W_in = x.size(4);
    int Cout = weight.size(1);
    int K = weight.size(2);
    int D_out = (D_in - 1) * stride - 2 * padding + dilation * (K - 1) + 1;
    int H_out = (H_in - 1) * stride - 2 * padding + dilation * (K - 1) + 1;
    int W_out = (W_in - 1) * stride - 2 * padding + dilation * (K - 1) + 1;
    auto out = torch::zeros({B, Cout, D_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());
    if (stride == 2 && padding == 1 && dilation == 2 && K == 3) {
        int D_odd = D_out / 2;
        int H_odd = H_out / 2;
        int W_odd = W_out / 2;
        int total = B * Cout * D_odd * H_odd * W_odd;
        const int threads = 256;
        const int blocks = (total + threads - 1) / threads;
        conv_transpose3d_forward_specialized_kernel<3><<<blocks, threads>>>(
            x.data_ptr<float>(), weight.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>(),
            B, Cin, Cout, D_in, H_in, W_in, D_out, H_out, W_out);
    } else {
        int total = B * Cout * D_out * H_out * W_out;
        const int threads = 256;
        const int blocks = (total + threads - 1) / threads;
        conv_transpose3d_forward_generic_kernel<<<blocks, threads>>>(
            x.data_ptr<float>(), weight.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>(),
            B, Cin, Cout, D_in, H_in, W_in, D_out, H_out, W_out,
            K, (int)stride, (int)padding, (int)dilation);
    }
    return out;
}
"""

if torch.cuda.is_available():
    module = load_inline(
        name="conv_transpose3d_fast",
        cpp_sources="",
        cuda_sources=cuda_sources,
        functions=["conv_transpose3d_forward"],
        extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3"],
        verbose=False,
    )
else:
    module = None

class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, stride=1, padding=0, dilation=1, bias=False):
        super().__init__()
        self.conv_transpose3d = nn.ConvTranspose3d(
            in_channels, out_channels,
            kernel_size=(kernel_size, kernel_size, kernel_size),
            stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, bias=bias
        )

    def forward(self, x):
        if module is None or not x.is_cuda:
            return self.conv_transpose3d(x)
        x = x.contiguous()
        weight = self.conv_transpose3d.weight.contiguous()
        stride = self.conv_transpose3d.stride[0] if isinstance(self.conv_transpose3d.stride, tuple) else self.conv_transpose3d.stride
        padding = self.conv_transpose3d.padding[0] if isinstance(self.conv_transpose3d.padding, tuple) else self.conv_transpose3d.padding
        dilation = self.conv_transpose3d.dilation[0] if isinstance(self.conv_transpose3d.dilation, tuple) else self.conv_transpose3d.dilation
        out = module.conv_transpose3d_forward(x, weight, stride, padding, dilation)
        if self.conv_transpose3d.bias is not None:
            out += self.conv_transpose3d.bias.view(1, -1, 1, 1, 1)
        return out
